kubeRegistry is a wrapper around a prometheus registry-type object. Upon initialization\n   214→// the kubernetes binary version information is loaded into the registry object, so that\n   215→// automatic behavior can be configured for metric versioning.\n   216→type kubeRegistry struct {\n   217→\tPromRegistry\n   218→\tversion              semver.Version\n   219→\thiddenCollectors     map[string]Registerable // stores all collectors that has been hidden\n   220→\tstableCollectors     []StableCollector       // stores all stable collector\n   221→\thiddenCollectorsLock sync.RWMutex\n   222→\tstableCollectorsLock sync.RWMutex\n   223→\tresetLock            sync.RWMutex\n   224→\tresettables          []resettable\n   225→}\n   226→\n   227→// Register registers a new Collector to be included in metrics\n   228→// collection. metrics in it.\n   373→// Since we can not register a metrics twice, so we have to unregister first then register again.\n   374→func (kr *kubeRegistry) enableHiddenStableCollectors() {\n   375→\tif 392→\tkr.CustomMustRegister(cs...)\n   393→}\n   394→\n   395→// Reset invokes Reset on all metrics that are resettable.\n   396→func (kr *kubeRegistry) Reset() {\n   397→\tkr.resetLock.RLock()\n   398→\tdefer kr.resetLock.RUnlock()\n   399→\tfor _, r := range kr.resettables {\n   400→\t\tr.Reset()\n   401→\t}\n   402→}\n   403→\n   404→// BuildVersion is a helper function that can be easily Upon initialization\n// the kubernetes binary version information is loaded into the registry object, so that\n// automatic behavior can be configured for metric versioning.\ntype kubeRegistry struct {\n\tPromRegistry\n\tversion              semver.Version\n\thiddenCollectors     map[string]Registerable // stores all collectors that has been hidden\n\tstableCollectors     []StableCollector       // stores all stable collector\n\thiddenCollectorsLock sync.RWMutex\n\tstableCollectorsLock sync.RWMutex\n\tresetLock            sync.RWMutex\n\tresettables          []resettable\n}\n\n// Register registers a new Collector to be included in metrics\n// collection. It returns an error if the descriptors provided by the\n// Collector are invalid or if they — in combination with descriptors of\n// already registered Collectors — do not fulfill the consistency and\n// uniqueness criteria described in the documentation of metric.Desc.\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) Register(c Registerable) error {\n\tif c.Create(&kr.version) {\n\t\tdefer kr.addResettable(c)\n\t\treturn kr.PromRegistry.Register(c)\n\t}\n\n\tkr.trackHiddenCollector(c)\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Registerer exposes the underlying prometheus.Registerer\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) Registerer() prometheus.Registerer {\n\treturn kr.PromRegistry\n}\n\n// Gatherer exposes the underlying prometheus.Gatherer\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) Gatherer() prometheus.Gatherer {\n\treturn kr.PromRegistry\n}\n\n// MustRegister works like Register but registers any number of\n// Collectors and panics upon the first registration that causes an\n// error.\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) MustRegister(cs ...Registerable) {\n\tmetrics := make([]prometheus.Collector, 0, len(cs))\n\tfor _, c := range cs {\n\t\tif c.Create(&kr.version) {\n\t\t\tmetrics = append(metrics, c)\n\t\t\tkr.addResettable(c)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tkr.trackHiddenCollector(c)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tkr.PromRegistry.MustRegister(metrics...)\n}\n\n// CustomRegister registers a new custom collector.\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) CustomRegister(c StableCollector) error {\n\tkr.trackStableCollectors(c)\n\tdefer kr.addResettable(c)\n\tif c.Create(&kr.version, c) {\n\t\treturn kr.PromRegistry.Register(c)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// CustomMustRegister works like CustomRegister but registers any number of\n// StableCollectors and panics upon the first registration that causes an\n// error.\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) CustomMustRegister(cs ...StableCollector) {\n\tkr.trackStableCollectors(cs...)\n\tcollectors := make([]prometheus.Collector, 0, len(cs))\n\tfor _, c := range cs {\n\t\tif c.Create(&kr.version, c) {\n\t\t\tkr.addResettable(c)\n\t\t\tcollectors = append(collectors, c)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tkr.PromRegistry.MustRegister(collectors...)\n}\n\n// RawMustRegister takes a native prometheus.Collector and registers the collector\n// to the registry. This bypasses metrics safety checks, so should only be used\n// to register custom prometheus collectors.\n//\n// Deprecated\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) RawMustRegister(cs ...prometheus.Collector) {\n\tkr.PromRegistry.MustRegister(cs...)\n\tfor _, c := range cs {\n\t\tkr.addResettable(c)\n\t}\n}\n\n// addResettable will automatically add our metric to our reset\n// list if it satisfies the interface\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) addResettable(i interface{}) {\n\tkr.resetLock.Lock()\n\tdefer kr.resetLock.Unlock()\n\tif resettable, ok := i.(resettable); ok {\n\t\tkr.resettables = append(kr.resettables, resettable)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Unregister unregisters the Collector that equals the Collector passed\n// in as an argument.  (Two Collectors are considered equal if their\n// Describe method yields the same set of descriptors.) The function\n// returns whether a Collector was unregistered. Note that an unchecked\n// Collector cannot be unregistered (as its Describe method does not\n// yield any descriptor).\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) Unregister(collector Collector) bool {\n\treturn kr.PromRegistry.Unregister(collector)\n}\n\n// Gather calls the Collect method of the registered Collectors and then\n// gathers the collected metrics into a lexicographically sorted slice\n// of uniquely named MetricFamily protobufs. Gather ensures that the\n// returned slice is valid and self-consistent so that it can be used\n// for valid exposition. As an exception to the strict consistency\n// requirements described for metric.Desc, Gather will tolerate\n// different sets of label names for metrics of the same metric family.\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) Gather() ([]*dto.MetricFamily, error) {\n\treturn kr.PromRegistry.Gather()\n}\n\n// trackHiddenCollector stores all hidden collectors.\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) trackHiddenCollector(c Registerable) {\n\tkr.hiddenCollectorsLock.Lock()\n\tdefer kr.hiddenCollectorsLock.Unlock()\n\n\tkr.hiddenCollectors[c.FQName()] = c\n\thiddenMetricsTotal.Inc()\n}\n\n// trackStableCollectors stores all custom collectors.\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) trackStableCollectors(cs ...StableCollector) {\n\tkr.stableCollectorsLock.Lock()\n\tdefer kr.stableCollectorsLock.Unlock()\n\n\tkr.stableCollectors = append(kr.stableCollectors, cs...)\n}\n\n// enableHiddenCollectors will re-register all of the hidden collectors.\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) enableHiddenCollectors() {\n\tif len(kr.hiddenCollectors) == 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tkr.hiddenCollectorsLock.Lock()\n\tcs := make([]Registerable, 0, len(kr.hiddenCollectors))\n\n\tfor _, c := range kr.hiddenCollectors {\n\t\tc.ClearState()\n\t\tcs = append(cs, c)\n\t}\n\n\tkr.hiddenCollectors = make(map[string]Registerable)\n\tkr.hiddenCollectorsLock.Unlock()\n\tkr.MustRegister(cs...)\n}\n\n// enableHiddenStableCollectors will re-register the stable collectors if there is one or more hidden metrics in it.\n// Since we can not register a metrics twice, so we have to unregister first then register again.\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) enableHiddenStableCollectors() {\n\tif len(kr.stableCollectors) == 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tkr.stableCollectorsLock.Lock()\n\n\tcs := make([]StableCollector, 0, len(kr.stableCollectors))\n\tfor _, c := range kr.stableCollectors {\n\t\tif len(c.HiddenMetrics()) > 0 {\n\t\t\tkr.Unregister(c) // unregister must happens before clear state, otherwise no metrics would be unregister\n\t\t\tc.ClearState()\n\t\t\tcs = append(cs, c)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tkr.stableCollectors = nil\n\tkr.stableCollectorsLock.Unlock()\n\tkr.CustomMustRegister(cs...)\n}\n\n// Reset invokes Reset on all metrics that are resettable.\nfunc (kr *kubeRegistry) Reset() {\n\tkr.resetLock.RLock()\n\tdefer kr.resetLock.RUnlock()\n\tfor _, r := range kr.resettables {\n\t\tr.Reset()\n\t}\n}\n\n// BuildVersion is a helper function that can be easily mocked.\nvar BuildVersion = version.Get\n\nfunc newKubeRegistry(v apimachineryversion.Info) *kubeRegistry {\n\tr := &kubeRegistry{\n\t\tPromRegistry:     prometheus.NewRegistry(),\n\t\tversion:          parseVersion(v),\n\t\thiddenCollectors: make(map[string]Registerable),\n\t\tresettables:      make([]resettable, 0),\n\t}\n\n\tregistriesLock.Lock()\n\tdefer registriesLock.Unlock()\n\tregistries = append(registries, r)\n\n\treturn r\n}\n\n// NewKubeRegistry creates a new vanilla Registry\nfunc NewKubeRegistry() KubeRegistry {\n\tr := newKubeRegistry(BuildVersion())\n\treturn r\n}\n\nfunc (r *kubeRegistry) RegisterMetaMetrics() kubernetes/kubernetes, grafana/grafana, and prometheus/prometheus, three distinct yet complementary patterns for Prometheus metric registration and exposure emerge:\\n\\n## Kubernetes: Custom Registry with Version Awareness\\n\\nKubernetes implements the most sophisticated pattern through a **custom KubeRegistry wrapper** (kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go). The KubeRegistry interface wraps prometheus.Registry and adds version-aware registration:\\n\\n- **Registerable interface** requires metrics to implement Create(version), ClearState(), and FQName() methods, enabling version-based hiding and deprecation tracking\\n- **kubeRegistry.Register()** and **kubeRegistry.MustRegister()** check version compatibility before registration, automatically tracking deprecated metrics\\n- **Custom metric types** (Counter, Gauge, Histogram, Summary) in counter.go, gauge.go, and histogram.go implement the Registerable interface with stability levels (STABLE, BETA, ALPHA)\\n\\nThe legacyregistry/registry.go file provides a global default registry instance with factory functions (MustRegister, RawMustRegister) for backward compatibility. The init() function registers native Prometheus collectors (ProcessCollector, GoCollector) using RawMustRegister, demonstrating how Kubernetes integrates Prometheus stdlib collectors.\\n\\n## Grafana: Layered Registration with Wrapper Patterns\\n\\nGrafana (grafana/grafana:pkg/infra/metrics/metrics.go) takes a **declarative approach with layered wrappers**:\\n\\n- Metrics are declared as package-level variables (MInstanceStart, MPageStatus, MApiStatus, etc.) across multiple types: Counter, CounterVec, Gauge, GaugeVec, Summary, SummaryVec, Histogram\\n- The **init() function** (lines 262-718) explicitly creates all metrics using prometheus.NewCounter(), prometheus.NewGauge(), etc., with options like Namespace=\\\"grafana\\\" and Help text\\n- **initMetricVars()** function (line 785) calls prometheus.Registerer.MustRegister() for batch registration\\n- **ProvideService()** (pkg/infra/metrics/service.go) is a dependency injection point that initializes metrics during service startup by calling initMetricVars(reg)\\n\\nGrafana additionally wraps the Kubernetes legacyregistry (imported as k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry) through:\\n- **ProvideRegisterer()** returns legacyregistry.Registerer() to use Kubernetes' global registry\\n- **addPrefixWrapper** (service.go) modifies metric names to add \\\"grafana_\\\" prefix\\n- **NewMultiRegistry()** combines multiple gatherers (k8s and Prometheus default) with a deny-list for conflicts\\n\\nThis pattern shows Grafana's adoption of Kubernetes' metrics infrastructure while maintaining its own metrics namespace.\\n\\n## Prometheus: Direct Registration with Factory Patterns\\n\\nPrometheus (prometheus/prometheus:cmd/prometheus/main.go) uses **direct global registration** with a factory pattern for composable metrics:\\n\\n- Package-level variables (configSuccess, configSuccessTime) defined at lines 131-138 using prometheus.NewGauge()\\n- **init() function** (line 147) calls prometheus.MustRegister(versioncollector.NewCollector(...)), demonstrating early registration\\n- Metrics are registered at init-time before main() executes\\n\\nFor modular metric registration, Prometheus implements a **Metrics struct factory pattern** (discovery/metrics.go):\\n- **NewManagerMetrics(registerer, sdManagerName)** creates a Metrics struct containing Counter, Gauge, and GaugeVec fields\\n- Each metric is created individually (prometheus.NewGauge, prometheus.NewCounter) and stored in struct fields\\n- Metrics are registered via **registerer.Register()** in a loop, with error handling\\n- **Unregister()** method enables cleanup, essential for temporary discovery managers\\n\\nThis pattern enables dependency injection of registrers and lazy initialization of metric groups.\\n\\n## Key Differences\\n\\n1. **Registration Time**: Kubernetes uses version-aware delayed registration; Grafana uses init-time declarative setup; Prometheus uses init-time direct registration\\n2. **Scope**: Kubernetes provides a stable, abstract registry interface; Grafana layers wrappers over it; Prometheus uses the default global registry\\n3. **Composability**: Kubernetes handles deprecation internally; Grafana provides dependency injection through ProvideService; Prometheus provides factory functions for metric groups\\n4. **Integration**: Kubernetes' legacyregistry serves as the underlying infra for both Kubernetes and Grafana; Prometheus stands independently with direct prometheus/client_golang (kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go). The KubeRegistry interface wraps prometheus.Registry and adds version-aware registration:\\n\\n- **Registerable interface** requires metrics to implement Create(version), ClearState(), and FQName() methods, enabling version-based hiding and deprecation tracking\\n- **kubeRegistry.Register()** and **kubeRegistry.MustRegister()** check version compatibility before registration, automatically tracking deprecated metrics\\n- **Custom metric types** (Counter, Gauge, Histogram, Summary) in counter.go, gauge.go, and histogram.go implement the Registerable interface with stability levels (STABLE, BETA, ALPHA)\\n\\nThe legacyregistry/registry.go file provides a global default registry instance with factory functions (MustRegister, RawMustRegister) for backward compatibility. The init() function registers native Prometheus collectors (ProcessCollector, GoCollector) using RawMustRegister, demonstrating how Kubernetes integrates Prometheus stdlib collectors.\\n\\n## Grafana: Layered Registration with Wrapper Patterns\\n\\nGrafana (grafana/grafana:pkg/infra/metrics/metrics.go) takes a **declarative approach with layered wrappers**:\\n\\n- Metrics are declared as package-level variables (MInstanceStart, MPageStatus, MApiStatus, etc.) across multiple types: Counter, CounterVec, Gauge, GaugeVec, Summary, SummaryVec, Histogram\\n- The **init() function** (lines 262-718) explicitly creates all metrics using prometheus.NewCounter(), prometheus.NewGauge(), etc., with options like Namespace=\\\"grafana\\\" and Help text\\n- **initMetricVars()** function (line 785) calls prometheus.Registerer.MustRegister() for batch registration\\n- **ProvideService()** (pkg/infra/metrics/service.go) is a dependency injection point that initializes metrics during service startup by calling initMetricVars(reg)\\n\\nGrafana additionally wraps the Kubernetes legacyregistry (imported as k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry) through:\\n- **ProvideRegisterer()** returns legacyregistry.Registerer() to use Kubernetes' global registry\\n- **addPrefixWrapper** (service.go) modifies metric names to add \\\"grafana_\\\" prefix\\n- **NewMultiRegistry()** combines multiple gatherers (k8s and Prometheus default) with a deny-list for conflicts\\n\\nThis pattern shows Grafana's adoption of Kubernetes' metrics infrastructure while maintaining its own metrics namespace.\\n\\n## Prometheus: Direct Registration with Factory Patterns\\n\\nPrometheus (prometheus/prometheus:cmd/prometheus/main.go) uses **direct global registration** with a factory pattern for composable metrics:\\n\\n- Package-level variables (configSuccess, configSuccessTime) defined at lines 131-138 using prometheus.NewGauge()\\n- **init() function** (line 147) calls prometheus.MustRegister(versioncollector.NewCollector(...)), demonstrating early registration\\n- Metrics are registered at init-time before main() executes\\n\\nFor modular metric registration, Prometheus implements a **Metrics struct factory pattern** (discovery/metrics.go):\\n- **NewManagerMetrics(registerer, sdManagerName)** creates a Metrics struct containing Counter, Gauge, and GaugeVec fields\\n- Each metric is created individually (prometheus.NewGauge, prometheus.NewCounter) and stored in struct fields\\n- Metrics are registered via **registerer.Register()** in a loop, with error handling\\n- **Unregister()** method enables cleanup, essential for temporary discovery managers\\n\\nThis pattern enables dependency injection of registrers and lazy initialization of metric groups.\\n\\n## Key Differences\\n\\n1. **Registration Time**: Kubernetes uses version-aware delayed registration; Grafana uses init-time declarative setup; Prometheus uses init-time direct registration\\n2. **Scope**: Kubernetes provides a stable, abstract registry interface; Grafana layers wrappers over it; Prometheus uses the default global registry\\n3. **Composability**: Kubernetes handles deprecation internally; Grafana provides dependency injection through ProvideService; Prometheus provides factory functions for metric groups\\n4. **Integration**: Kubernetes' legacyregistry serves as the underlying infra for both Kubernetes and Grafana; Prometheus stands independently with direct prometheus/client_golang usage\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
